 Whenever songs are mentioned in the history of Hindi cinema, a name definitely appears in golden letters, that is Mohammad Rafi
 aaj rafee sahab kaa janmdin he
 a funk that people still remember through his songs
 chaahe neeche ke sur ho yaa upar vaale geet, mohammad rafee ko har tarah ke geet gane main maharath hasil thi
 Apart from Hindi, Mohammed Rafi has sung songs in Assamese, Konkani, Bhojpuri, Odia, Punjabi, Bengali, Marathi, Sindhi, Kannada, Gujarati, Telugu, Maghi, Maithili, Urdu, as well as English, Persian, Arabic and Dutch languages
 , Let's know some special things about Mohammed Rafi Sahab
 
 
 1
 Mohammad Rafiqa was born on 24 December 1924 in Amritsar (punjab)
 ek vakt ke baad rafee sahab ke pita apane parivaar ke saath lahore chale gaye the
 2
 mohammad rafee kaa nik nem 'fico' tha or bachapan se hi raah chalate fakiron ko sunate hue rafee sahab ne gaanaa shuru kar diya tha
 3
 mohammad rafee ne ustad abdul vaahid khan, pandit jivan laal mattu or firoz nijaami se shastreey sangeet kii shiksha lee thi
 4
 maatr 13 saal kii umr menmohammad rafee ne lahoremein us jamaane ke mashhoor abhinayta 'ke el sahagal' ke gaanon ko gaakar public parformens di thi
 5
 rafee sahab ne sabase pehle lahore main punjabi film 'gul baloch' ke liye 'soniye ni, hiriye ni' gaanaa gaaya tha
 6
 mohammad rafee ne mumbai aakar saal 1944 main pehali baar hindi film ke liye geet gaaya tha
 The name of the film was 'village Ki Gori'
 7
 Mohammed Rafi was considered a compassionate singer, as he never mentioned the fees for the song and sometimes even gave the song for 1 rupee
 8
 Mohammed Rafi has sung the most duet songs with 'asha Bhosle'
 rafee saab ne singer kishor kumaar ke liye bhi unki do filmon 'bade sarkaar' or 'raagini' main aawaaj di thi
 9
 mohammad rafee ko 'kya hua tera vaad' gane ke liye 'neshnal aword' se sammanit kiya gaya tha
 In 1967, he was also awarded the 'padma Shri' award from the Government of India
 10
 Mohammed Rafi died on 31 July 1980 due to a heart attack and according to reports it was raining heavily that day
 rafee sahab ke dehanth par mashhoor geetkaar naushaad ne likhaa, 'goonjte he teri aawaaj amiron ke mahal main, jhopadon kii garibon main bhi he tere saaj, yun to apni mausiki par sabko fakr hota he magar e mere saathi mausiki ko bhi aaj tujh par naaj he
 Four days ago in the capital Delhi, the case of a dead body found in the forest has been resolved by the police
 yuvak kii hatya udhaar ke paise na chukaane kii vajah se kii gai thi
 Police has arrested three people, including a minor, in this regard
 south east dilli ke ambedkar nagar ilaake main chaar din pehle jangal se police ko ek yuvak kii jali huilashmili thi
 The police was engaged in solving the case since then
 shanivaar ko police ne hatya ke is maamle se pardaa hataa diya
 Police said that on January 10, a half-dead body was found in the forest of Ambedkar Nagar
 yuvak kii hatya kar uski laash ko jalaane ke baad jangal main phenk diya gaya tha
 The deceased was identified as Chetan
 police ke mutabik chetan ne dedh saal pehle vikram se 35 hazaar rupee udhaar liye the
 But he was not paying the loan money
 isi baat par vikram ne suraj ke saath milakar uskihatyaki saazish rachi
 Under which Chetan was first drunk
 phir uske sir main rod maar kar uski hatya kar di gai
 After this, the corpse was burnt and thrown into the forest to mislead the police
 rashtriya rajdhani dilli main shelter home kii kami ke chalate lagaataar ho rahi mauton ko lekar daakhil janhit yachika par hoicourt ne dilli sarkaar ko notice jari kiya he
 The court has asked the government to file its reply in four weeks
 ab maamle kii agali sunwaayee chaar may ko hogi
 The petition filed in the Delhi High Court argued that many times anti-social elements in the shelter home molest women and children
 saath hi beghar hone kii vajah se police inaki report bhi darj nahin karti he
 Therefore, women, girls and children below 12 years should be given separate home shelters
 iske alaava shelter home kam hone ke kaaran dilli main 2004 se 2015 ke bich 34 hazaar se zyada log footpath or sadakon par apni jaan ganvaa chuke hai
 From 1 to 19 January, 119 homeless died in 2016, between 1 and 18 January 140 homeless people died on the streets in the bitter cold
 yachika main ye bhi kaha gaya he ki ek se 19 janvari 2017 ke bich 119 logo kii maut thand se thithur kar sadako par hui
 The petition states that people are dying on the roads every year due to lack of shelter home in Delhi as per the requirement
 jab disambar-janvari kii sardi or may-june kii garmi apane charam par hoti he, to yah aankada kaaphi bad jaataa he
 Many petitions have been done before, the High Court has already heard on many petitions regarding the lack of shelter home in sunavaidilli
 saath hi kai sakht aadesh bhi sarkaar ko die gaye, lekin iske baavjood bhi sthiti main kuch khaas sudhaar nahin aayaa
 The High Court also showed seriousness in this matter, because the eyes cannot be closed on the deaths of over 34 thousand in 11 years in the country's capital
 khaas kar tab jab ise rokane kii sarkaar eemaandaaree se koshish nahin kar rahi he
 His girlfriend has registered a rape case against Deepak Chakraborty, principal of CMD College in Bilaspur, Chhattisgarh
 praathmik jaanch ke baad police ne dfa 376 ke tahat FIR darj kar lee he
 The victim alleged that the accused raped her by giving her a cold cold drink and also blackmailed her by making a video of her
 aaropee bilaspur ke siemdi college ke praachaarya deepak chakravarti hai
 It is being told that Deepak also does parttime RCM business
 bilaspur ke sarkanda ilaake main ek flats unka daftar bhi he
 The 45-year-old victim has been associated with him for the last several years
 donon kaa aksar milanaa julna rahata tha
 The woman alleged that in August 2017, when she went to work in Deepak Chakravarti's flat in Sarakanda, he fraudulently drank and raped her by mixing drugs in cold drinks
 is dauraan aaropee praachaarya ne mahila kaa video bhi banaaya
 When the woman regains consciousness, she comes to know about the incident
 deepak ne mahila ko munh kholane par video viral kar dene kii dhamkee di
 After this, he started blackmailing her continuously
 peedit mahila ke mutabik praachaarya aae din use apane sarkanda sthit flats main bulaakar usase shaareerik sambandh banaata tha
 Fearing slander, she could not tell this thing to anyone
 magar ek din pareshaan hokar aakhirkaar usne is baat kii shikaayat police thane main darj kara di
 However, the accused principal Deepak has described the allegations of the complainant as false
 unke mutabik yah mahila kaaphi samay se unase moti rakam kii maang kar rahi thi
 At present, the police is investigating the case
 maamla darj ho jane ke baad se aaropee praachaarya deepak chakravarti apane awaas se faraar he
 Let us know that CMD College is one of the largest colleges in Bilaspur
 jahaan dhai hajaar ke lagbhag vidhyaarthee padhate hai
 The college staff is also surprised by the case of the rape of the college principal
 jo log sangharsh, utpeedan yaa maanavadhikaron ke ulanghan ke kaaran sharnaarthi banakar jivan kaat rahe hai, unke liye awaas, kapade or bhojan kaa intjaam karne par zyaadaatar dhyaan diya jaataa he, lekin duniya ke kareeb chah karod sharnaarthiyon ko salanaa kam se kam 27
 8 lakh surgeries are also needed
 ek shodh se yah jaankaree mili he
 The head of the research team, Adam Kushner of Baltimore's John Hapkings Bloomberg School of Public Health, says, "we are facing one of the biggest refugee crises since World War II, forcing refugees to become refugees
" ' kushaner aage kehete hai, 'bimariyon ke ilaaj ke liye surgery behad jaruri he, lekin sankat ke samay is par dhyaan nahin diya jaataa
 Due to lack of timely surgery, many people become crippled and many die
 ' This research has been published online in the World Journal of Surgery
 shodhakartaaon ne sharnaarthiyon ko madad muhaiyaa karaane vaale kuch sarkaron or maanviya sahaayta sanghathanon ko unki surgery sambandhi aavashyaktaaon par prakaash daalaa he
 "when refugees are planned to help, the focus is on providing housing, food and clothing for them, but surgery is also a basic need that no one talks about," says Kushner
 ' Refugees mostly require surgery to remove hernia, broken bones, caesareans, cleft lips, and gallbladder
 iske alaava jalane ke nishaan or taankon ko hataane kii surgery kii jarurat hoti he
 For this research, researchers collected data on the number of refugees worldwide, internally displaced people and asylum seekers, and their demographics from the United Nations High Commissioner for Refugees (UNHCR) and the United Nations Palestinian Refugee Relief and Action Agency in the Near East
 shodhakartaaon ne prati varsh aavashyak surgery kii sankhya kaa anumaan lagane ke liye purv main prakashit is aankade kaa istemaal kiya, jisamen prati 100,000 aabaadi par vaarshik taur par nunatam 4,669 surgery kii jarurat hoti he
 The comments shodh main kaha gaya he ki inamen se zyaadaatar sharnaarthi unke liye banaae gaye shiviron main rahete hai
 Most refugees are unable to get it done due to lack of proper documents, high cost of surgery and weak surgery structure in the host country
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 This is published directly from the Syndicate feed)
 shodh dal ke pramukh balteemor ke jon hapakings bloomvarg skool of public health ke adam kushaner kaa kahana he, 'ham dwitiya vishwayuddh ke baad se sabase bade sharnaarthi sankat se jujh rahe hai, jo majaboor hokar sharnaarthi bane hai
 'kushner further adds,' Surgery is very important for the treatment of diseases, but it is not taken care of in times of crisis
 samay par surgery kii suvidha nahin milane se kai log aapng ho jate hai to kai log mar jate hai
 ' yah shodh world jarnal of surgery main online prakashit kiya gaya he
 Researchers have highlighted some of the surgery and humanitarian aid organizations that provide help to refugees for their surgery needs
 kushaner kehete hai, 'jab sharnaarthiyon kii madad kii yojana banaai jaati he to sara dhyaan unke liye awaas, bhojan or kapade muhaiyaa karaane par hota he, lekin surgery bhi ek buniyadi jarurat he, jiske bare main koi baat nahin karata
 ' sharnaarthiyon ko zyaadaatar hernia, tuuti haddiyaan, sijerian, phank vaale hoth or pittashay kii thili hataane kii surgery kii jarurat hoti he
 Also surgery to remove burn marks and stitches is required
 is shodh ke liye shodhakartaaon ne duniya bhar main sharnaarthiyon kii sankhya, aatanrik rup se visthapit logon or sharan chaahane waalon par or unki janasankhyikee par sanyukt raashtra sharnaarthi ucchayukta (yuanechasiaar) or niyar east main sanyukt raashtra philistini sharnaarthi raahat evam kaary agency se aankade jutaaye
 Researchers used this previously published figure to estimate the number of surgeries required per year, requiring a minimum of 4,669 surgeries per 100,000 population annually
 tippaniyan Research says that most of these refugees live in camps built for them
 zyaadaatar sharnaarthi uchit dastavejon kii kami, surgery kii oonchi laagat or mejabaan desh main surgery ke kamjor dhaanche ke kaaran ise karvaa nahin pate hai

 What is guide lines
 
 
 - sookhaa or geela kooda alag-alag karen
 Wet waste is organic, including cooked or uncooked food items
 jabaki sookhe kooday main plastic, rabar, metal jaisi chizein shaamil hai
 Another part of the garbage from the waste is hazardous litter, which includes paints, pesticides, cleaning agents and their containers
 -kooday ke sahi niptaan ke liye jaruri he ki geela kooda yani jo biodigradable he use alag dibbe main daalaa jaae
 The MCD has set a green box for this
 - saath hi sookhe kooday ke liye nile dibbe kaa istemaal kiya janaa chahie
 Rubber, metal or plastic waste should be added to it
 -geele or sookhe kooday ko mix nahin kiya janaa chahie
 Hazardous garbage should also be disposed of separately
 -houseing societiz main geele or sookhe kooday ke liye alag-alag bade dustbin south emsidi lagaaegi
 In this, the waste will be dumped according to the color of dustbin, this waste will be collected everyday by the staff of South MCD at a fixed time
 -geela kooda rozaana uthaaya jayega, jabaki sookhaa kooda teen din main ek baar uthaaya jayega
 Also, the garbage falling in the dangerous category will be picked up once a week and transported to the designated places
 -balk garbej utpaadan karne vaale sansthaanon yaa sarkari buildigon main garbej composter lagane kaa niyam banaaya jayega, jisamen garbej process kiya jayega
 But until the composter is put in place, the housing society rules will also apply to bulk garbage generators
 -geela yaa sookhaa kisi bhi tarah kaa kooda khule maidan yaa sadak kinare phenkna gaiyrkanoonee hoga
